and I went more to the field of research</span></li><ul class="listtype-bullet listindent2 list-bullet2"><li><span class=" author-d-1gg9uz65z1iz85zgdz68zmqkz84zo2qovw8ywz84zz80zwz89z0pz80zuybiz70z6oyz71zx3z72zz90zsz81zz82z7e7z85z">I wanted to explore something that is now interesting - that now everyone is using</span></li></ul><li><span class=" author-d-1gg9uz65z1iz85zgdz68zmqkz84zo2qovw8ywz84zz80zwz89z0pz80zuybiz70z6oyz71zx3z72zz90zsz81zz82z7e7z85z">And I've seen that the whole field of Cloud and APIs and all these things - it's really going to be the hottest thing now: APIs have started to take up a lot of space now in our lives</span></li><ul class="listtype-bullet listindent2 list-bullet2"><li><span class=" author-d-1gg9uz65z1iz85zgdz68zmqkz84zo2qovw8ywz84zz80zwz89z0pz80zuybiz70z6oyz71zx3z72zz90zsz81zz82z7e7z85z">Between apps, between apps and DBs, between Clients and Servers - and so I started . . .</span></li><li><span class=" author-d-1gg9uz65z1iz85zgdz68zmqkz84zo2qovw8ywz84zz80zwz89z0pz80zuybiz70z6oyz71zx3z72zz90zsz81zz82z7e7z85z">Then I joined the research team at </span><span class="attrlink url author-d-1gg9uz65z1iz85zgdz68zmqkz84zo2qovw8ywz84zz80zwz89z0pz80zuybiz70z6oyz71zx3z72zz90zsz81zz82z7e7z85z"><a class="attrlink" data-target-href="https://nonamesecurity.com/" href="https://nonamesecurity.com/" rel="noreferrer nofollow noopener" target="_blank">noname</a></span></li><ul class="listtype-bullet listindent2 list-bullet2"><li><span class=" author-d-1gg9uz65z1iz85zgdz68zmqkz84zo2qovw8ywz84zz80zwz89z0pz80zuybiz70z6oyz71zx3z72zz90zsz81zz82z7e7z85z">And the company - its goal is to make API Security, when the product gives you three things:</span></li><li><span class=" author-d-1gg9uz65z1iz85zgdz68zmqkz84zo2qovw8ywz84zz80zwz89z0pz80zuybiz70z6oyz71zx3z72zz90zsz81zz82z7e7z85z">One is the visibility on your APIs - usually, if you went to corporate CISOs or people like that, and you said to him,</span><span class=" author-d-1gg9uz65z1iz85zgdz68zmqkz84zo2qovw8ywz84zz80zwz89z0pz80zuybiz70z6oyz71zx3z72zz90zsz81zz82z7e7z85z s-quot"> </span><span class=" author-d-1gg9uz65z1iz85zgdz68zmqkz84zo2qovw8ywz84zz80zwz89z0pz80zuybiz70z6oyz71zx3z72zz90zsz81zz82z7e7z85z h-quot">"Say,</span><span class=" author-d-1gg9uz65z1iz85zgdz68zmqkz84zo2qovw8ywz84zz80zwz89z0pz80zuybiz70z6oyz71zx3z72zz90zsz81zz82z7e7z85z"> how many APIs do you have?" - he doesn't know, he's not sure about it.</span></li><li><span class=" author-d-1gg9uz65z1iz85zgdz68zmqkz84zo2qovw8ywz84zz80zwz89z0pz80zuybiz70z6oyz71zx3z72zz90zsz81zz82z7e7z85z">"Which one do credit cards go through?" or</span><span class=" author-d-1gg9uz65z1iz85zgdz68zmqkz84zo2qovw8ywz84zz80zwz89z0pz80zuybiz70z6oyz71zx3z72zz90zsz81zz82z7e7z85z s-quot"> </span><span class=" author-d-1gg9uz65z1iz85zgdz68zmqkz84zo2qovw8ywz84zz80zwz89z0pz80zuybiz70z6oyz71zx3z72zz90zsz81zz82z7e7z85z h-quot">"In</span><span class=" author-d-1gg9uz65z1iz85zgdz68zmqkz84zo2qovw8ywz84zz80zwz89z0pz80zuybiz70z6oyz71zx3z72zz90zsz81zz82z7e7z85z"> what authentications?" - any use of APIs, even if we say, in the most familiar and broad use, it is a programmer who builds some kind of Web application and people access it through the browser or through their phone, and then basically there are all kinds of APIs that return to you information that the app requests or that the browser requests.</span></li><ul class="listtype-bullet listindent2 list-bullet2"><li><span class=" author-d-1gg9uz65z1iz85zgdz68zmqkz84zo2qovw8ywz84zz80zwz89z0pz80zuybiz70z6oyz71zx3z72zz90zsz81zz82z7e7z85z">Then it is displayed on the screen, for the user.</span></li><li><span class=" author-d-1gg9uz65z1iz85zgdz68zmqkz84zo2qovw8ywz84zz80zwz89z0pz80zuybiz70z6oyz71zx3z72zz90zsz81zz82z7e7z85z">So these are the most recognizable APIs . . .</span></li></ul></ul><div><span class=" author-d-1gg9uz65z1iz85zgdz68zmqkz84zo2qovw8ywz84zz80zwz89z0pz80zuybiz70z6oyz71zx3z72zz90zsz81zz82z7e7z85z">(Ran) ok . . . Anyway, we're talking about</span><span class=" author-d-1gg9uz65z1iz85zgdz68zmqkz84zo2qovw8ywz84zz80zwz89z0pz80zuybiz70z6oyz71zx3z72zz90zsz81zz82z7e7z85z s-quot"> </span><span class=" author-d-1gg9uz65z1iz85zgdz68zmqkz84zo2qovw8ywz84zz80zwz89z0pz80zuybiz70z6oyz71zx3z72zz90zsz81zz82z7e7z85z h-quot">"over-the-network",</span><span class=" author-d-1gg9uz65z1iz85zgdz68zmqkz84zo2qovw8ywz84zz80zwz89z0pz80zuybiz70z6oyz71zx3z72zz90zsz81zz82z7e7z85z"> right? We’re not talking about internal things, which happen </span><span class=" author-d-1gg9uz65z1iz85zgdz68zmqkz84zo2qovw8ywz84zz80zwz89z0pz80zuybiz70z6oyz71zx3z72zz90zsz81zz82z7e7z85z"><i>inside </i></span><span class=" author-d-1gg9uz65z1iz85zgdz68zmqkz84zo2qovw8ywz84zz80zwz89z0pz80zuybiz70z6oyz71zx3z72zz90zsz81zz82z7e7z85z">the process?</span></div><ul class="listtype-bullet listindent1 list-bullet1"><li><span class=" author-d-1gg9uz65z1iz85zgdz68zmqkz84zo2qovw8ywz84zz80zwz89z0pz80zuybiz70z6oyz71zx3z72zz90zsz81zz82z7e7z85z">(Eliad) So no - it's not those APIs . . . It's Web-APIs, it's APIs that go through the computer itself.</span></li></ul><div><span class=" author-d-1gg9uz65z1iz85zgdz68zmqkz84zo2qovw8ywz84zz80zwz89z0pz80zuybiz70z6oyz71zx3z72zz90zsz81zz82z7e7z85z">(Ori) Okay, not </span><span class="attrlink url author-d-1gg9uz65z1iz85zgdz68zmqkz84zo2qovw8ywz84zz80zwz89z0pz80zuybiz70z6oyz71zx3z72zz90zsz81zz82z7e7z85z"><a class="attrlink" data-target-href="https://youtu.be/L_o_O7v1ews?t=15" href="https://youtu.be/L_o_O7v1ews?t=15" rel="noreferrer nofollow noopener" target="_blank">inside the computer</a></span><span class=" author-d-1gg9uz65z1iz85zgdz68zmqkz84zo2qovw8ywz84zz80zwz89z0pz80zuybiz70z6oyz71zx3z72zz90zsz81zz82z7e7z85z"> itself - but it could be that . . . they immediately wanted to talk to investors and get investments and financings and all that, and then they didn't have a name yet.</span></li><ul class="listtype-bullet listindent2 list-bullet2"><li><span class=" author-d-1gg9uz65z1iz85zgdz68zmqkz84zo2qovw8ywz84zz80zwz89z0pz80zuybiz70z6oyz71zx3z72zz90zsz81zz82z7e7z85z">And in the emails they sent to investors, they wrote to them that</span><span class=" author-d-1gg9uz65z1iz85zgdz68zmqkz84zo2qovw8ywz84zz80zwz89z0pz80zuybiz70z6oyz71zx3z72zz90zsz81zz82z7e7z85z s-quot"> </span><span class=" author-d-1gg9uz65z1iz85zgdz68zmqkz84zo2qovw8ywz84zz80zwz89z0pz80zuybiz70z6oyz71zx3z72zz90zsz81zz82z7e7z85z h-quot">"It's</span><span class=" author-d-1gg9uz65z1iz85zgdz68zmqkz84zo2qovw8ywz84zz80zwz89z0pz80zuybiz70z6oyz71zx3z72zz90zsz81zz82z7e7z85z"> a </span><span class=" author-d-1gg9uz65z1iz85zgdz68zmqkz84zo2qovw8ywz84zz80zwz89z0pz80zuybiz70z6oyz71zx3z72zz90zsz81zz82z7e7z85z"><i>noname </i></span><span class=" author-d-1gg9uz65z1iz85zgdz68zmqkz84zo2qovw8ywz84zz80zwz89z0pz80zuybiz70z6oyz71zx3z72zz90zsz81zz82z7e7z85z">API Security company" - So that's the name.</span></li></ul></ul><div><span class=" author-d-1gg9uz65z1iz85zgdz68zmqkz84zo2qovw8ywz84zz80zwz89z0pz80zuybiz70z6oyz71zx3z72zz90zsz81zz82z7e7z85z">(Ran) It's good that they didn't put &lt;triangular brackets&gt;, as they usually do - it was very difficult to pronounce it...</span></div><div><span class=" author-d-1gg9uz65z1iz85zgdz68zmqkz84zo2qovw8ywz84zz80zwz89z0pz80zuybiz70z6oyz71zx3z72zz90zsz81zz82z7e7z85z">&nbsp;</span></div><div><span class=" author-d-1gg9uz65z1iz85zgdz68zmqkz84zo2qovw8ywz84zz80zwz89z0pz80zuybiz70z6oyz71zx3z72zz90zsz81zz82z7e7z85z">Ok, so look - we have quite a few things that we're going to talk about and we won't be able to talk about the whole security world of APIs, so let's pick a few things here.</span></div><div><span class=" author-d-1gg9uz65z1iz85zgdz68zmqkz84zo2qovw8ywz84zz80zwz89z0pz80zuybiz70z6oyz71zx3z72zz90zsz81zz82z7e7z85z">Let's start with this: I'm now creating an outward-facing API and I want to secure it. that's not good enough.</span></li></ul><li><span class=" author-d-1gg9uz65z1iz85zgdz68zmqkz84zo2qovw8ywz84zz80zwz89z0pz80zuybiz70z6oyz71zx3z72zz90zsz81zz82z7e7z85z">There are a few ways you can deal with this</span></li><ul class="listtype-bullet listindent2 list-bullet2"><li><span class=" author-d-1gg9uz65z1iz85zgdz68zmqkz84zo2qovw8ywz84zz80zwz89z0pz80zuybiz70z6oyz71zx3z72zz90zsz81zz82z7e7z85z">One of them is</span><span class="attrlink url author-d-1gg9uz65z1iz85zgdz68zmqkz84zo2qovw8ywz84zz80zwz89z0pz80zuybiz70z6oyz71zx3z72zz90zsz81zz82z7e7z85z"><a class="attrlink" data-target-href="https://authy.com/what-is-2fa/" href="https://authy.com/what-is-2fa/" rel="noreferrer nofollow noopener" target="_blank"> Two Factor Authentication</a></span><span class="attrlink url author-d-1gg9uz65z1iz85zgdz68zmqkz84zo2qovw8ywz84zz80zwz89z0pz80zuybiz70z6oyz71zx3z72zz90zsz81zz82z7e7z85z s-lparen"><a class="attrlink" data-target-href="https://authy.com/what-is-2fa/" href="https://authy.com/what-is-2fa/" rel="noreferrer nofollow noopener" target="_blank"> </a></span><span class="attrlink url author-d-1gg9uz65z1iz85zgdz68zmqkz84zo2qovw8ywz84zz80zwz89z0pz80zuybiz70z6oyz71zx3z72zz90zsz81zz82z7e7z85z h-lparen"><a class="attrlink" data-target-href="https://authy.com/what-is-2fa/" href="https://authy.com/what-is-2fa/" rel="noreferrer nofollow noopener" target="_blank">(2FA)</a></span></li><li><span class=" author-d-1gg9uz65z1iz85zgdz68zmqkz84zo2qovw8ywz84zz80zwz89z0pz80zuybiz70z6oyz71zx3z72zz90zsz81zz82z7e7z85z">The idea is that if someone eventually both obtained the username and the password - the attackers somehow got them - they still won't be able to log in to the account, because an SMS message still needs to be sent to that person's phone, and they need to confirm the login.</span></li><ul class="listtype-bullet listindent3 list-bullet3"><li><span class=" author-d-1gg9uz65z1iz85zgdz68zmqkz84zo2qovw8ywz84zz80zwz89z0pz80zuybiz70z6oyz71zx3z72zz90zsz81zz82z7e7z85z">This already prevents them from gaining access to the same account.</span></li></ul><li><span class=" author-d-1gg9uz65z1iz85zgdz68zmqkz84zo2qovw8ywz84zz80zwz89z0pz80zuybiz70z6oyz71zx3z72zz90zsz81zz82z7e7z85z">Today there are also more advanced protocols - one of them is </span><span class="attrlink url author-d-1gg9uz65z1iz85zgdz68zmqkz84zo2qovw8ywz84zz80zwz89z0pz80zuybiz70z6oyz71zx3z72zz90zsz81zz82z7e7z85z"><a class="attrlink" data-target-href="https://auth0.com/docs/authenticate/single-sign-on" href="https://auth0.com/docs/authenticate/single-sign-on" rel="noreferrer nofollow noopener" target="_blank">SSO,</a></span><span class=" author-d-1gg9uz65z1iz85zgdz68zmqkz84zo2qovw8ywz84zz80zwz89z0pz80zuybiz70z6oyz71zx3z72zz90zsz81zz82z7e7z85z"> </span><span class="attrlink url author-d-1gg9uz65z1iz85zgdz68zmqkz84zo2qovw8ywz84zz80zwz89z0pz80zuybiz70z6oyz71zx3z72zz90zsz81zz82z7e7z85z"><a class="attrlink" data-target-href="https://auth0.com/docs/authenticate/single-sign-on" href="https://auth0.com/docs/authenticate/single-sign-on" rel="noreferrer nofollow noopener" target="_blank">which is Single-Sign-On</a></span></li><ul class="listtype-bullet listindent3 list-bullet3"><li><span class=" author-d-1gg9uz65z1iz85zgdz68zmqkz84zo2qovw8ywz84zz80zwz89z0pz80zuybiz70z6oyz71zx3z72zz90zsz81zz82z7e7z85z">And the reference here is to a completely new concept, which really changed this world - it basically means that there is no more username and password for every site</span></li><li><span class=" author-d-1gg9uz65z1iz85zgdz68zmqkz84zo2qovw8ywz84zz80zwz89z0pz80zuybiz70z6oyz71zx3z72zz90zsz81zz82z7e7z85z">There's one</span><span class=" author-d-1gg9uz65z1iz85zgdz68zmqkz84zo2qovw8ywz84zz80zwz89z0pz80zuybiz70z6oyz71zx3z72zz90zsz81zz82z7e7z85z s-ldquo"> </span><span class=" author-d-1gg9uz65z1iz85zgdz68zmqkz84zo2qovw8ywz84zz80zwz89z0pz80zuybiz70z6oyz71zx3z72zz90zsz81zz82z7e7z85z h-ldquo">“major</span><span class=" author-d-1gg9uz65z1iz85zgdz68zmqkz84zo2qovw8ywz84zz80zwz89z0pz80zuybiz70z6oyz71zx3z72zz90zsz81zz82z7e7z85z"> website” which acts as the</span><span class=" author-d-1gg9uz65z1iz85zgdz68zmqkz84zo2qovw8ywz84zz80zwz89z0pz80zuybiz70z6oyz71zx3z72zz90zsz81zz82z7e7z85z s-quot"> </span><span class=" author-d-1gg9uz65z1iz85zgdz68zmqkz84zo2qovw8ywz84zz80zwz89z0pz80zuybiz70z6oyz71zx3z72zz90zsz81zz82z7e7z85z h-quot">"identity</span><span class=" author-d-1gg9uz65z1iz85zgdz68zmqkz84zo2qovw8ywz84zz80zwz89z0pz80zuybiz70z6oyz71zx3z72zz90zsz81zz82z7e7z85z"> manager" - it’s actually listed by all the people</span></li><li><span class=" author-d-1gg9uz65z1iz85zgdz68zmqkz84zo2qovw8ywz84zz80zwz89z0pz80zuybiz70z6oyz71zx3z72zz90zsz81zz82z7e7z85z">Everyone logs in to it and everyone has a username and password - and usually it's also with </span><span class="attrlink url author-d-1gg9uz65z1iz85zgdz68zmqkz84zo2qovw8ywz84zz80zwz89z0pz80zuybiz70z6oyz71zx3z72zz90zsz81zz82z7e7z85z"><a class="attrlink" data-target-href="https://authy.com/what-is-2fa/" href="https://authy.com/what-is-2fa/" rel="noreferrer nofollow noopener" target="_blank">Two Factor Authentication</a></span><span class=" author-d-1gg9uz65z1iz85zgdz68zmqkz84zo2qovw8ywz84zz80zwz89z0pz80zuybiz70z6oyz71zx3z72zz90zsz81zz82z7e7z85z"> so it's also very difficult to steal your identity from there</span></li><li><span class=" author-d-1gg9uz65z1iz85zgdz68zmqkz84zo2qovw8ywz84zz80zwz89z0pz80zuybiz70z6oyz71zx3z72zz90zsz81zz82z7e7z85z">And any other website you visit will actually verify your identity with that third-party site.</span></li><li><span class=" author-d-1gg9uz65z1iz85zgdz68zmqkz84zo2qovw8ywz84zz80zwz89z0pz80zuybiz70z6oyz71zx3z72zz90zsz81zz82z7e7z85z">Let's say, if Facebook is now the identity provider and I want to log in to another app - then you'll see a button for</span><span class=" author-d-1gg9uz65z1iz85zgdz68zmqkz84zo2qovw8ywz84zz80zwz89z0pz80zuybiz70z6oyz71zx3z72zz90zsz81zz82z7e7z85z s-quot"> </span><span class=" author-d-1gg9uz65z1iz85zgdz68zmqkz84zo2qovw8ywz84zz80zwz89z0pz80zuybiz70z6oyz71zx3z72zz90zsz81zz82z7e7z85z h-quot">"Sign-in</span><span class=" author-d-1gg9uz65z1iz85zgdz68zmqkz84zo2qovw8ywz84zz80zwz89z0pz80zuybiz70z6oyz71zx3z72zz90zsz81zz82z7e7z85z"> with Facebook" and there's actually some process where Facebook verifies my identity - it will be my verification for that site, and not the username and password for that site.</span></li></ul></ul></ul><div><span class=" author-d-1gg9uz65z1iz85zgdz68zmqkz84zo2qovw8ywz84zz80zwz89z0pz80zuybiz70z6oyz71zx3z72zz90zsz81zz82z7e7z85z">&nbsp;</span></div><div><span class=" author-d-1gg9uz65z1iz85zgdz68zmqkz84zo2qovw8ywz84zz80zwz89z0pz80zuybiz70z6oyz71zx3z72zz90zsz81zz82z7e7z85z">(Ran) So maybe there is not a single SSO Provider - I mean it's not just Facebook, there are a few more of them in the world - you can choose whether it's Facebook or Google or Twitter or LinkedIn or Whatever, But there are some big ones - and by and large each user chooses where to manage their identities, and of course you don't have to choose once but you can choose for each site someone else.</span></div><div><span class=" author-d-1gg9uz65z1iz85zgdz68zmqkz84zo2qovw8ywz84zz80zwz89z0pz80zuybiz70z6oyz71zx3z72zz90zsz81zz82z7e7z85z">But what does it mean?
